CREATE TABLE discs(
	disc_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
	product_id,
	cd_pn,
	case_pn,
	date,
	name,
	note,
	ordinal,
	filename,
	contributor,
	attachment,
	date_added,
	havefile,
	havetar,
	product_disc_num
);
